Default: 0.55\n\n    The noise variance schedule is defined as:\n        sigma^2 = eta / (1 + t)^gamma\n    where t is the step count (starting from 0).\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        optimizer: Optimizer,\n        eta: float = 0.01,\n        gamma: float = 0.55,\n    ) -> None:\n        if not isinstance(optimizer, Optimizer):\n            raise TypeError(f\"{type(optimizer).__name__} is not an Optimizer\")\n        if eta < 0.0:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Invalid eta value: {eta}\")\n        if gamma < 0.0:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Invalid gamma value: {gamma}\")\n\n        self.optimizer = optimizer\n        self.eta = eta\n        self.gamma = gamma\n        self._step_count = 0\n\n    def __getattr__(self, name: str) -> Any:\n        \"\"\"Forward attribute access to the wrapped optimizer.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            return getattr(self.optimizer, name)\n        except AttributeError:\n            raise AttributeError(\n                f\"'{type(self).__name__}' object has no attribute '{name}'\"\n            )\n\n    def step(self, closure: Optional[Callable[[], float]] = None) -> Optional[float]:\n        r\"\"\"Perform a single optimization step with gradient noise injection.\n\n        Args:\n            closure (callable, optional): A closure that reevaluates the model and returns the loss.\n\n        Returns:\n            The loss value if closure is provided, otherwise None.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Inject noise before the optimizer step\n        self._inject_noise()\n\n        # Call the base optimizer's step\n        loss = self.optimizer.step(closure)\n\n        # Increment step count for next iteration\n        self._step_count += 1\n\n        return loss\n\n    def _inject_noise(self) -> None:\n        r\"\"\"Inject Gaussian noise into gradients with decaying variance.\"\"\"\n        # Calculate noise variance: sigma^2 = eta / (1 + t)^gamma\n        variance = self.eta / ((1 + self._step_count) ** self.gamma)\n        std = variance ** 0.5\n\n        # Inject noise to all parameters that have gradients\n        for group in self.optimizer.param_groups:\n            for param in group[\"params\"]:\n                if param.grad is not None:\n                    # Add Gaussian noise scaled by the standard deviation\n                    noise = torch.randn_like(param.grad) * std\n                    param.grad.add_(noise)\n\n    def state_dict(self) -> dict[str, Any]:\n        r\"\"\"Return the state of the wrapper and wrapped optimizer.\"\"\"\n        return {\n            \"optimizer_state_dict\": self.optimizer.state_dict(),\n            \"step_count\": self._step_count,\n            \"eta\": self.eta,\n            \"gamma\": self.gamma,\n        }\n\n    def load_state_dict(self, state_dict: dict[str, Any]) -> None:\n        r\"\"\"Load the state of the wrapper and wrapped optimizer.\"\"\"\n        self.optimizer.load_state_dict(state_dict[\"optimizer_state_dict\"])\n        self._step_count = state_dict.get(\"step_count\", 0)\n        self.eta = state_dict.get(\"eta\", 0.01)\n        self.gamma = state_dict.get(\"gamma\", 0.55)\n\n    def zero_grad(self, set_to_none: bool = True) -> None:\n        r\"\"\"Zero the gradients of the wrapped optimizer.\"\"\"\n        self.optimizer.zero_grad(set_to_none=set_to_none)\n\n    def __repr__(self) -> str:\n        return (\n            f\"{self.__class__.__name__}(\\n\"\n            f\"  optimizer={self.optimizer},\\n\"\n            f\"  eta={self.eta},\\n\"\n            f\"  gamma={self.gamma},\\n\"\n            f\")\"\n        )\n","numLines":119,"startLine":1,"totalLines":119}}}
